***verhangen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhangen.html>verhangen</a> (20192)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhangen.html>verhangen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cause to hang, to hang</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang somewhere else</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang someone (to execute by hanging)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hang oneself (to commit suicide by hanging)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verhuegen</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhuizen.html>verhuizen</a> (2135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, or <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huizen.html>huizen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verhuizen.html>verhuizen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to move from one residence to another</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

***verkeer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkeer.html>verkeer</a> (3461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Verkehr</i>. Equivalent to a deverbal from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkeren.html>verkeren</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkeer.html>verkeer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">traffic</span></li>
<li>exchange, intercourse</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkering.html>verkering</a> (7613)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkeren.html>verkeren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">make out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkering.html>verkering</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkering.html>verkeringen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkering.html>verkerinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The state of having a relationship, of going out together.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nl:Bram_Bakker" class="extiw" title="w:nl:Bram Bakker">Bram <a href = vnd.unilang:bakker.html>Bakker</a></a>, “Dikke <a href = vnd.unilang:billen.html>billen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:nou.html>nou</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a>?”, in: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dwarse.html>dwarse</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:psychiater.html>psychiater</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgeverij.html>Uitgeverij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maart.html>Maarten</a> Muntinga, Amsterdam, →ISBN, p. 168
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:denken.html>denken</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoon.html>zoon</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vertelde.html>vertelde</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dertien.html>dertien</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verkering.html>verkering</a></b>.
<dl><dd>It reminds <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> of something my son <a href = vnd.unilang:told.html>told</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>. He <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thirteen and goes with a girl for the first time.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verkering.html>verkering</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onze.html>onze</a> overbuur.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She's in a <b>relationship</b> with our neighbour across the road.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Since it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mainly used for children and youth, it <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a connotation of not being very serious or long-lasting. Once it turns out to be more serious, one would use one of the synonyms, such as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:relatie.html>relatie</a></i>, or speak of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boyfriend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vriendin.html>vriendin</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">girlfriend</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>commonly collocates with <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***verkiezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezen.html>verkiezen</a> (17432)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verkiesen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">farkiesan</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kiezen.html>kiezen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezen.html>verkiezen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to prefer</li>
<li>to elect</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezen.html>verkiezen</a></b>

***verkiezing.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezing.html>verkiezing</a> (6397)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verkiesinge</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezen.html>verkiezen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezing.html>verkiezing</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezingen.html>verkiezingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verkiezing.html>verkiezinkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">election</span> (by vote or ballot)</li>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verklappen.html>verklappen</a></strong>
</p>
